Like the 1911, no handgun collection is complete without one. The open top slide design allows for easy clearing of rare jams. It fits great even in my small hands &amp; points dead-on naturally. Accuracy of the three I've owned equaled that of most 9mm competitors. The balance, weight, grip, &amp; pointability makes this a very pleasant, fun pistol to shoot all day.</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Curt</span> from <span class="Text"> NW Oregon</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> Best hand gun made</span>, April 28, 2011</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> Absolutely love my 92 fs 9mm it's the perfect weight it shoots accurate and smooth beats the hell out of my dads Glock 9mm</div> <div class="Row"> By <span class="Text"> Johnnyboy</span> from <span class="Text"> Texas</span></div> </div> </div> </td> </tr><tr> <td class="ReviewItem"> <div class="ItemStyle"> <div class="Title"> <span class="Subject"> Fits like a glove</span>, December 29, 2010</div> <div class="Content"> <div class="StarRating"> <img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"><img src="/themes/New5/Images/Star.gif" valign="absmiddle" alt="" border="0"></div> <div class="Row"> This is the first and only handgun I have ever owned.
